< review>
I stumbled into this place because it was nearby a lunchtime appointment. I loved the space. It was a mix between small tables and huge communal tables. It was very rustic and open. There were a lot of pre-packaged salads, but I was drawn to the sandwiches. I had the deviled egg salad sandwich. It had great, hearty bread that really held the egg salad and tomatoes in place. Great flavors. I'm interested to try more.</review>

< text>
Ambience: Great indoor and outdoor seating areas. You can bring your dogs there as well on a beautiful day.

Service: Okay friendly staff.

Food: I had corn flaked fried chicken sandwich. It was really tasty and has a crisp crunch to it.

Definitely will go back again with my dog. There are a lot of dogs passing by, so make sure that your dog will remain calm, so you and the people around you can have a pleasant meal.< /text>

< Text>
BIG FREAKING SANDWICHES. Tastes amazing. I absolutely love the fried chicken sandwich. There are 2 huge pieces of chicken and amazing tasting coleslaw. I like the Sloppy Joe sandwich, got good flavor has nice crunch because of the chips on top. Also the sriracha chicken salad sandwich is pretty amazing. (Yeah I eat a lot of chicken).

It comes with side. I always get house made chips, nicely seasoned and freshly made. Their mashed potatoes are pretty awesome too.

The reason for taking away one star is because out of 10 times I have been there, 2-3 times the food didnt taste great - maybe different chefs(?). Not sure. But again rest 8 times it was amazing. A must try if you are in the area.< /Text>

< text>
Came here for brunch on a Sunday because I'd heard good things about the brunch. It was OK.  I ordered the baked eggs, which I found to be mediocre.  My friend also ordered the baked eggs and there was a stark contrast between what she got and what I got. From what I could tell, my portion was substantially larger but was missing all of these veggies that hers had. Very inconsistent. Also, the latte I ordered was so horrible that I could barely take a sip. I just left it and didn't bother. Don't think I'd go again since there are plenty of other great brunch places in Potrero Hill.< /text>

I have a 2012 Jeep Wrangler with an P0420 engine code I've been clearing for the past year. It's up for smog so I needed to get it fixed. Other shops hymned and hawed at diagnosing the issue. Not these guys! Ryan(the Owner) answered the phone, I explained my situation and he told me, no problem, bring it in!

The part wasn't available till next day, which would cramp my plans. Ryan jumped on the phone and called half a dozen places and got the part coming same day. < review>
This location is experiencing growing pains at least I hope.

Food quality was on par to other CFAs so the star rating is relative to better experiences.

Arrived at the start of lunch time rush, line inside was only halfway to the door but still only had two cashiers working. 10 mins to put in order and 16 mins to receive food, seems like the norm as there were plenty of people sitting and waiting for their food. By the time I left, line was to the door and drive thru line had overflowed onto the street, which along with blocking traffic also blocks those that just want to park in the parking lot.

I plan to reassess in the future to see if improvements have been made.

4/14/20 Update: while their setup for curbside pick up, I beat the lunch time rush and my order came out incorrect. Ordered and paid for spicy chicken sandwich but received an original chicken sandwich< /review>
